שם ד"ה מגלה פנים (הב'): שכופר במה שכותב בתורה: [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx).
קט, א אויר מגדל משכח: [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).

**English:**

## Sanhedrin

9b [The opinion of Rav Yosef that one who is liable for a payment to one party and a payment to another is liable even for a single act]: [7](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/7.aspx).
11a One who is worthy of the Shechinah resting upon him, like Moshe Rabbeinu (and Gilyon HaShas): [41](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/41.aspx).
Regarding Hillel HaZaken... "He was a Chassid, he was an anav..." Shmuel HaKatan... "He was a Chassid, he was an anav": [41](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/41.aspx).
Shmuel HaKatan... "He also said..." (and Rashi: The Shechinah rested upon him, for he prophesied...): [44](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/44.aspx).
In Chiddushei Aggados Maharsha (regarding the opinion of Rabbi Yehuda bar Ilai that humility is greater than them all): Humility leads to Ruach HaKodesh: [40](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/40.aspx).
24a Torah scholars in Bavel who sharpen one another in Halacha: [46](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/46.aspx).
"He has made me dwell in darkness..." refers to the Talmud of Bavel: [46](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/46.aspx).
39a Wherever ten are gathered, the Shechinah resides: [43](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/43.aspx).
56a and onwards [regarding the mitzvos of a Ben Noach — between man and Hashem and between man and his fellow]: [135](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/1/135.aspx).
60a Kilayim (for a Ben Noach)... "Your beast you shall not let mate"... and also your field through grafting (and Rashi s.v. *Sadecha*): [96](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/2/96.aspx).
83a In Rashi s.v. *Terumah Chutz LaAretz*: This (tevel) is terumah mixed within it: [68](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/68.aspx).
Tevel... the verse speaks of those who are destined to separate terumah: [68](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/68.aspx).
83b Rav said: One who eats terumah is (only) liable for lashes: [66](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/66.aspx).
97a Three things come through a lack of awareness (hesech hada'as)... Mashiach: [89](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/1/89.aspx). [101](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/3/101.aspx).
98a In a generation that is entirely righteous...: [167](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/167.aspx).
"When will the Master come?"... "Today, if you will listen to His voice": [100](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/3/100.aspx). [198](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/198.aspx).
99a "For he has despised the word of Hashem..." one who breaks His covenant... and one who interprets the Torah in a distorted manner... (and "casting off the yoke" is not mentioned): [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx). [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
99b Menashe... would expound upon derogatory aggados... interpreting the Torah in a distorted manner: [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx).
In Rashi s.v. *Megaleh Panim* (the first): He acts brazenly...: [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx).
Ibid. s.v. *Megaleh Panim* (the second): He denies what is written in the Torah: [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx).
109a The air of Migdal causes forgetfulness: [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).

5b: If they killed, they are not executed [130](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/130.aspx).
10a: Words of Torah, etc., offer refuge [131](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/131.aspx).
11b: And he does not go out, etc., and even a Yisrael needs him, and even... like Yoav, etc. (and in the commentaries on the Mishnah) [127](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/127.aspx).
He went outside its boundary intentionally, etc., the redeemer of blood has permission, etc. (according to the version of the Rambam) [129](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/129.aspx).

13b: Rabbi Yitzchak says: those liable to Kares, etc. [67](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/67.aspx).
These words... but death and lashes, etc., Rava said: he warned him, etc. [67](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/67.aspx).
16a: But there is the pledge of a convert, etc. [71](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/71.aspx).

## שבועות

_Section: שבועות_

**Hebrew:**

יג, א כי דבר ה' בזה זה הפורק עול ומגלה פנים בתורה: [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx).
ברש"י ד"ה מגלה פנים: בא על ד"ת בחוצפה ובגלוי עזות פניו: 55­54.
שם: כגון מנשה שהי' יושב ודורש באגדות של דופי: [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).

**English:**

## Shavuos

13, a. "For he has despised the word of Hashem" — this refers to one who casts off the yoke and interprets the Torah in a brazen manner.

Rashi, s.v. *megaleh panim*: He approaches words of Torah with chutzpah and with an open display of insolence. 

Ibid.: For example, Menashe, who would sit and expound upon the Aggadah in a disparaging manner.

---

28a [If the *makshah* (beaten work) is an impediment even for future generations]: [34](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/34.aspx).

## חולין

5a, Rashi: One who performs idol worship denies Hashem: [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
91b and onwards (that the Ofanim say, "Blessed is the glory of Hashem from His place"): [121](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/121.aspx).
129a: When one has used an object of wood, he has performed a service: [201](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/8/201.aspx).
130b: A Levi who ate his tithes while they were still tevel... they are exempt from payment... you have nothing regarding them except from the time of the separation [of the tithe] and onwards: [70](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/70.aspx).

## ספרי

###### שלח

טו, כב וכי תשגו . . ע"ז . . מה העובר . . אף ע"ז שפורק עול ומפר ברית ומגלה פנים בתורה: [53](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/53.aspx). [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).

בספרי דבי רב: [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
טו, כג את כל אשר צוה . . אף כו' שנא' מן היום כו' כל המודה בע"ז כו': [53](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/53.aspx).
טו, ל מגלה פנים בתורה כמנשה . . שהי' דורש בהגדה של דופי כו': [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx). [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
טו, לא כי דבר ה' בזה זה המגלה פנים בתורה: [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx). [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).

###### קרח

יח, כ הכל במשמע כהנים לוים וישראלים . . בארצם לא תנחל יצאו כו': [103](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/103.aspx).
יח, כג ובתוך בנ"י לא ינחלו כו' שומע אני כו': [103](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/103.aspx).
יח, כד את מעשר בנ"י . . קראו המקום תרומה עד כו' (ובמפרשים): [68](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/68.aspx).
לפי שנא' ונשל . . אבל קני קניזי וקדמוני לא שמענו ת"ל על כן כו': [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).
יח, כט את מקדשו ממנו שאם נפל לתוכו ה"ה מקדשו מכאן אמרו כו': [60](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/60.aspx). [62](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/62.aspx).
יח, לב אם הפרשת אותו שלא מן המובחר כו': [65](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/65.aspx).
ואת קדשי . . ה"ז אזהרה לכהנים כו': [65](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/65.aspx).

###### חוקת

יט, טו וכל כלי . . בכלי חרס הכתוב מדבר . . רמ"א . . כלי שמקבל טומאה דרך פתוחו כו': [72](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/72.aspx).
חבית שכפאה על פי' כו' טמאה כו': [75](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/75.aspx).
כלי גללים . . אדמה מנין ודין הוא כו': [72](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/72.aspx).

###### פינחס

כו, נג הכל במשמע ישראל כהנים ולוים (ויש גי' בהסדר) . . יצאו כהנים כו': [103](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/103.aspx).

###### ראה

יא, כח מן הדרך . . מכאן אמרו כל המודה בע"ז ככופר בכל התורה כו': [56](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/56.aspx).

**English:**

###### Naso

6:3 "There is no *nezirah* anywhere except for *perishah* (abstinence)." [31](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/31.aspx).
6:11 "For having sinned..." He requires atonement for having afflicted his soul by abstaining from wine. [31](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/31.aspx).

###### Behaaloscha

10:33 "The way of the *atarim*..." It does not say *taryim* (spies), but rather... (according to the version of Rabbeinu Hillel and others). [78](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/2/78.aspx).
The way of the *atarim*... Aharon died... their great scout (*tayyar*). [78](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/2/78.aspx).

###### Shelach

15:22 "And if you err..." Regarding *avodah zarah*... Just as the one who transgresses [in other matters]... so too regarding *avodah zarah*, he casts off the yoke, breaks the covenant, and interprets the Torah in a distorted manner (*megaleh panim baTorah*). [53](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/53.aspx). [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
According to the commentary of Rabbeinu Hillel: *Megaleh panim baTorah* means that he brazenly defies the Torah by not fulfilling its precepts. [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx).
In *Sifrei d'bei Rav*: [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
15:23 "All that Hashem has commanded..." Even... as it is said, "from the day..." Anyone who acknowledges *avodah zarah*... [53](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/53.aspx).
15:30 *Megaleh panim baTorah* like Menashe... who would expound upon the *Aggadah* with slanderous intent... [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx). [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
15:31 "Because he has despised the word of Hashem"—this is one who *megaleh panim baTorah*. [54](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/54.aspx). [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).

###### Korach

18:20 "Everything" includes *kohanim*, *levi'im*, and *yisraelim*... "You shall have no inheritance in their land"—this excludes... [103](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/103.aspx).
18:23 "And in the midst of the Bnei Yisrael they shall have no inheritance..." I might infer... [103](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/103.aspx).
18:24 "The tithe of the Bnei Yisrael..." The *Makom* (Hashem) called it *terumah* until... (and in the commentaries). [68](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/68.aspx).
Because it is said, "And *venashal*..." But we have not heard of the *Keni*, *Kenizi*, and *Kadmoni*; the verse teaches, "Therefore..." [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).
18:29 "Its sanctified portion from it"—this implies that if [the non-sanctified] fell into it, it becomes sanctified; from here they said... [60](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/60.aspx). [62](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/62.aspx).
18:32 "If you set it apart not from the choicest..." [65](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/65.aspx).
"And you shall not profane the holy things..." This is a warning to the *kohanim*... [65](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/65.aspx).

###### Chukas

19:15 "And every vessel..." The verse speaks of an earthenware vessel... *Rema*... a vessel that receives *tumah* through its opening... [72](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/72.aspx).
A barrel that he turned over on its opening... is *tamei*... [75](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/75.aspx).
Vessels of dung... from where do we know [they are susceptible to *tumah*] regarding earth? It is a logical deduction... [72](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/72.aspx).

###### Pinchas

26:53 "Everything" includes *yisraelim*, *kohanim*, and *levi'im* (there is a version regarding the order)... *kohanim* are excluded... [103](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/103.aspx).

###### Re'eh

11:28 "From the way..." From here they said: Anyone who acknowledges *avodah zarah* is as one who denies the entire Torah... [56](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/56.aspx).

פ"כ, ג ויגר מואב . . למואבים נראו מזויינים . . מה שאתה יכול לחטוף כו': [87](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/1/87.aspx).
היו מתייראין . . בא סיחון . . הרי ארצנו לפניהם לכך היו מתייראין: [87](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/1/87.aspx).
פ"כ, ט בלעם . . שונא יותר מבלק: [86](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/1/86.aspx).

**English:**

## במדבר רבה

Chapter 20, 16: "Just as a young girl..." "...her parents do not complain..." "...so too are Yisrael, etc." 
End of Chapter 9: "Regarding the woman who goes astray..." "...under the Ribono shel Olam, His servant, etc." "...and the Ribono shel Olam is jealous for them, etc." 
Chapter 14, 12: Regarding the four elements. 
Chapter 15, 4: "Take this loaf of gold..." "...it is made by itself..." "...the final hammer blow, etc." 
"So he made the Menorah..." "...the Ribono shel Olam." 
Chapter 15, 10: "And you shall make a Menorah..." "...Moshe found it difficult..." "...Betzalel..." "...he made it." 
Chapter 16, 14: They did not want to take from the fruits of Eretz Yisrael, were it not for Calev. 
Chapter 19, 1: "A decree have I decreed, etc." 
Chapter 19, 4: "The face of Moshe turned pale, etc." 
Chapter 19, 20: "The way of the spies, the great scout..." "...as it is stated: 'And the Ark of the Covenant of Hashem traveled before them'." 
"Amalek was always like a strap of chastisement for Yisrael, etc." 
Chapter 20, 3: "And Moav feared..." "...to the Moavites they appeared armed..." "...whatever you can snatch, etc." 
"They were afraid..." "...Sichon came..." "...'Behold, our land is before them,' therefore they were afraid." 
Chapter 20, 9: "Bilam..." "...he hated more than Balak." 
Chapter 20, 19: "Who can count the mitzvos that they perform in the dust: 'You shall not plow'..." "...and likewise all of them." 
"You shall not plow..." "...for three years it shall be for you, etc." 
"You shall not sow your vineyard with diverse seeds."

## קהלת רבה

_Section: קהלת רבה_

**Hebrew:**

פ"א, ג שבע שבתות תמימות תהיינה אימתי בזמן שאין ישוע ושכני' ביניהם (ומ"כ בשם הרוקח): [8](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/8.aspx).

**English:**

## Koheles Rabbah

"Seven complete weeks shall they be" (Vayikra 23:15) — when are they "complete"? At a time when there is no *Yeshu* (ego) and *Shechinas* (the Divine Presence) among them (and so it is brought in the name of the *Rokeach*). [8]

היו מתייראין שראו כל הארץ ביד ישראל שבא סיחון . . ארצנו לפניהם כו': [87](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/1/87.aspx).
ה בלעם . . הי' שונא אותם יותר מבלק כו': [86](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/1/86.aspx).
יב מי יוכל למנות מצות שהם עושים בעפר לא תחרוש . . וכן כולם: [93](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/2/93.aspx). [95](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/2/95.aspx).

###### חוקת

מב מת התייר הגדול . . שנא' וארון ברית ה' כו': [78](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/2/78.aspx).

**English:**

## Tanchuma

### Tisa
21 And I descend at Sinai with My tetramorphs [146].

### Behaaloscha
3 Moshe was perplexed... "Take gold"... He would strike with a hammer and it would form itself [33]. [34].
"So Moshe did"—it does not say here [that Moshe did it], rather, who did it? Hashem [33]. [37].
6 "And you shall make a Menorah"... He was perplexed by it... Betzalel... immediately made it [33].

### Shelach
8 They did not want to take from the fruits of the land, were it not for Calev, etc. [48].

### Chukas
6 The face of Moshe turned pale, etc. [98].
18 "The way of the Atharim"—the great scout... as it is stated, "And the Ark of the Covenant of Hashem traveled before them"... to scout, etc. [78]. [79].
Amalek was always a strap of chastisement for Yisrael, etc. [81].

### Balak
2 "And Moav was afraid"... Yisrael appeared to the Moavites as armed... whatever you can seize, etc. [87].
They were afraid because they saw the entire land in the hands of Yisrael, for Sichon had come... "Our land is before them," etc. [87].
5 Bilam... hated them more than Balak, etc. [86].
12 "Who can count the mitzvos that they perform in the dust"—"You shall not plow," and so on for all of them [93]. [95].
"Three years it shall be forbidden to you" [92].
"You shall not sow your vineyard with diverse seeds" [95].

### Chukas
42 The great scout died... as it is stated, "And the Ark of the Covenant of Hashem," etc. [78].

**English:**

## Zohar

###### Part I

28a: "The Beis Hamikdash will be built by the hand of the Ribono shel Olam, etc." [39](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/39.aspx).
164a: "Through an arousal from below, there is an arousal from above." [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).
235a: "Through an arousal from below, there is an arousal from above." [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).
244a: "Through an arousal from below, there is an arousal from above." [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).

###### Part II

131a: [Fire flaming within the number of the kelipos]. [160](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/160.aspx).
183b: "When Yisroel went out... matzah... from here... and all the more so on the day of Shavuos (a korban of chametz)." [194](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/194.aspx).
219a-b: [Ketores is to remove the filth]. [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).

###### Part III

97a-b: "And you shall count for yourselves... like this woman... and she shall count for herself, so too here, etc." 14-15.
127b: "A nazir... is called holy... and the hair of his head... his locks, etc. (three levels)." [31](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/31.aspx).
149b: "A king... it is not his honor to speak the words of a commoner, etc." [43](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/43.aspx).
160b: "Kalev and Yehoshua took it... as it is written, 'And they carried it on a pole between two, etc.'" [48](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/48.aspx).
221a: "And for the time to come... the building of the Ribono shel Olam is what we await, and not the building of a human being, etc." [39](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/39.aspx).
257b: "For the Master of all, there is no division in Him, neither in names nor in letters, etc." [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).

###### Nusach HaTefillah

Birchos HaShachar: "Ashreinu, how good is our portion, etc." [223](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/12/223.aspx).
Haggadah Shel Pesach: "Had He brought us close before Har Sinai, etc." [139](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/1/139.aspx).

## יד החזקה

_Section: יד החזקה_

**Hebrew:**

[19](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/19.aspx) (הכותרות לההלכות הם ל' הרמב"ם). [30](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/30.aspx) (דרכו להעתיק דיני התלמוד כלשונם). [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx) (אין דרכו לכתוב ענינים מחודשים כו').
הקדמה הגמרא הבבלית . . אחר . . הגמרא הירושלמית בכמו מאה שנה: [45](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/45.aspx).
מצות עשה רמ"ח סימן להם מנין אבריו של אדם: [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

**English:**

## יד החזקה

[19](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/19.aspx) (The headings for the laws are the language of the Rambam). [30](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/30.aspx) (His approach is to copy the laws of the Gemara verbatim). [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx) (It is not his way to write novel concepts, etc.).
Introduction: The Babylonian Gemara . . after . . the Jerusalem Gemara by approximately one hundred years: [45](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/45.aspx).
The 248 positive mitzvos correspond to the number of a person’s limbs: [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

## הל' תשובה

_Section: הל' תשובה_

פ"א ה"א כשיעשה תשובה וישוב מחטאו חייב להתוודות כו': [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
פ"ב ה"ב ומה היא התשובה הוא שיעזוב החוטא כו' ויגמור בלבו כו': [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).

פ"ג הי"א וזהו הנק' מגלה פנים בתורה מפני שהעיז כו': [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).

פ"ז ה"ה [פסוק ושבת עד ה"א הוא הבטחה וסיפור דברים]: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).

**English:**

## הל' תשובה

The requirement that the sinner return from his sin before Hashem and confess: [19](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/19.aspx). [20](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/20.aspx).
Chapter 1, Halacha 1: When one performs teshuvah and returns from his sin, he is obligated to confess, etc.: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
Chapter 2, Halacha 2: And what is teshuvah? It is that the sinner abandons [his sin], etc., and resolves in his heart, etc.: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
That the sinner abandons [his sin], etc., and likewise feels regret for what he has done: [21](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/21.aspx).
To confess with his lips . . . that which he resolved in his heart: [19](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/19.aspx).
Chapter 2, Halacha 3: One who confesses with words but has not resolved in his heart to abandon [the sin], this is like one who immerses in a mikveh while holding a sheretz in his hand, etc.: [19](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/19.aspx).
Chapter 3, Halacha 11: And this is what is called "revealing faces in Torah," because he acted brazenly, etc.: [55](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/2/55.aspx).
Chapter 5: [The connection of the concept of . . . "free choice" to Hilchos Teshuvah]: [23](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/23.aspx).
Chapter 5, Halacha 3: A great principle, etc., and that is the Torah and the mitzvah: [23](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/23.aspx).
Chapter 5, Halacha 4: If . . . by which judgment . . . he is punished, etc.; therefore, etc.: [24](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/24.aspx).
Chapter 7, Halacha 5: [The verse "And you shall return unto Hashem" is both a promise and a statement of fact]: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).

**English:**

## Laws of Forbidden Foods

Chapter 10, Law 19: One who eats *tevel* before [it has been tithed]... is liable for death at the hands of Heaven, as it is stated, "And they cause them to bear..." [69](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/69.aspx).
Chapter 15, Law 15: Why did they rely on the measure of one hundred in *terumos*... as it is stated, "His sanctuary..." [60](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/60.aspx). [62](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/62.aspx).

## Laws of Shechita

Chapter 2, Law 20: But one who performs *shechita* for the sake of a *nazir's* burnt offering... for the essence of *nezirus* is a vow among [other] vows: [26](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/26.aspx).

## Laws of Vows

Chapter 1, Law 2: If he transgressed and shaved or... he is lashed... because of "He shall not profane..." [27](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/27.aspx).
Chapter 1, Law 10: The sin-offering and the guilt-offering... it is possible... that one who takes a vow of *nezirus* brings a sin-offering...: [26](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/26.aspx).

## Laws of Nezirus

Chapter 1, Law 1: *Nezirus* is a vow from the category of *nidrei issar* (prohibitory vows): [27](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/27.aspx).
Chapter 1, Law 5: This is a complete *nazir*... even though it was not in his heart to become a *nazir* except regarding this matter...: [30](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/30.aspx).
Chapter 2, Law 16: A *nochri* cannot become a *nazir*, as it is stated, "Speak to the Children of Israel": [30](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/30.aspx).
Chapter 3, Law 13: Shimshon... the angel separated him from ritual impurity: [32](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/32.aspx).
Chapter 4, Law 11: One who says, "I am a *nazir* on the day that the son of Dovid comes"...: [32](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/32.aspx).
Chapter 10, Law 14: One who vows to Hashem in a path of holiness, this is praiseworthy...: [27](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/27.aspx). [31](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/31.aspx).

Chapter 7, Law 12: One does not assess tzedakah for orphans, even, etc. [111](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/2/111.aspx). [115](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/2/115.aspx).

## הל' תרומות

_Section: הל' תרומות_

**Hebrew:**

פ"א ה"ב­ג א"י האמורה בכל מקום היא בארצות שכובשן מלך ישראל כו' הארצות שכבש כו': [105](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/105.aspx). [106](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/106.aspx).
פ"ג הי"ב תרו"מ . . יש לישראל להפריש אותה כו': [69](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/69.aspx).
פ"ד הט"ז ונחשב לכם . . במחשבה בלבד תהי' תרומה: [63](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/63.aspx).
פי"ג ה"א התרומה עולה באחד ומאה (ובנ"כ): [60](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/60.aspx).
פי"ג ה"י סאה תרומה שנפלה לפחות ממאה . . אם בשוגג כו': [62](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/62.aspx).
פי"ד ה"א אם אין ידוע אם שחורה היתה ואם לבנה עולה באחד ומאה מן הכל: [60](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/60.aspx).
פי"ד הכ"א איסור המדומע מדבריהן כו': [62](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/62.aspx).

**English:**

## Laws of Terumos

Chapter 1, Laws 2-3: The "Eretz Yisrael" mentioned everywhere refers to the lands conquered by a king of Yisrael, etc., the lands that he conquered, etc. [105](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/105.aspx). [106](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/106.aspx).

Chapter 3, Law 12: Terumos and Ma'asros... it is incumbent upon a Yisrael to separate them, etc. [69](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/69.aspx).

Chapter 4, Law 16: "And it shall be considered for you"... it shall be considered Terumah through thought alone. [63](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/63.aspx).

Chapter 13, Law 1: Terumah is nullified in one hundred and one (and in the commentaries). [60](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/60.aspx).

Chapter 13, Law 10: A se'ah of Terumah that fell into less than one hundred... if it was unintentional, etc. [62](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/62.aspx).

Chapter 14, Law 1: If it is unknown whether it was black or white, it is nullified in one hundred and one of the total. [60](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/60.aspx).

Chapter 14, Law 21: The prohibition of *meduma* is Rabbinic in origin, etc. [62](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/62.aspx).

**English:**

## Laws of Shemitah and Yovel

Chapter 13, Law 5: The tribe of Levi, etc., were commanded that Yisrael give them cities, etc., in the days of Moshiach, etc. [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).

Chapter 13, Law 10: The entire tribe of Levi is warned not to inherit land in the land of Canaan (and see Mishneh Lamelech): [103](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/103.aspx).

Chapter 13, Law 11: These matters apply only to land regarding which a covenant was made... and which was divided, etc.: [106](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/106.aspx). [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).

However... that which a king conquers... the Kohanim, etc., are [permitted]: [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx). [105](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/105.aspx).

In Radbaz (and Kesef Mishneh): And a verse supports this, etc.: [108](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/108.aspx).

Chapter 13, Law 12: And why did Levi not merit, etc.? "I am your portion and your inheritance": [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).

Chapter 13, Law 13: To be set apart to stand before Hashem, to serve Him and to worship Him... this person is, etc.: [5](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/1/1/5.aspx). [109](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/109.aspx).

Not only the tribe of Levi, etc., this person is sanctified as holy of holies, etc.: [225](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/12/225.aspx).

## ספר המצות

_Section: ספר המצות_

**Hebrew:**

הקדמה בסופו: רמ"ח (מצות) כנגד אבריו של אדם: [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).
שרש ג שאין ראוי למנות מצוות שאין נוהגין לדורות: [105](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/105.aspx).
שרש ד אין ראוי למנות הציוויים הכוללים התורה כולה: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
מ"ע עג שצונו להתודות על העונות כו': [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
מ"ע צד [נדר הוי בגדר חיוב גברא]: [29](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/29.aspx).
מ"ע קמ למנות השנים . . כמו שימנה כל איש ואיש ממנו ימי העומר: [15](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/15.aspx).
מל"ת קנג [ע"פ ואת קדשי בנ"י לא תחללו]: [66](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/66.aspx).
מל"ת קנז [נדר הוי בגדר חיוב גברא]: [29](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/29.aspx).
מל"ת קסט שלא יקח כל שבט לוי חלק בארץ: [105](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/105.aspx).
מל"ת קעט התילד עוף מעיפוש כו': [184](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/184.aspx).

**English:**

## Sefer HaMitzvos

Introduction at the end: The 248 (mitzvos) correspond to the limbs of a person: [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).
Root 3: That it is not appropriate to count mitzvos that do not apply for all generations: [105](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/105.aspx).
Root 4: It is not appropriate to count commandments that encompass the entire Torah: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
Positive Mitzvah 73: That we are commanded to confess our sins, etc.: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
Positive Mitzvah 94: [A vow is in the category of a personal obligation]: [29](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/29.aspx).
Positive Mitzvah 140: To count the years . . just as every individual among us counts the days of the Omer: [15](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/15.aspx).
Negative Mitzvah 153: [Based on "And you shall not profane the holy things of the Children of Israel"]: [66](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/66.aspx).
Negative Mitzvah 157: [A vow is in the category of a personal obligation]: [29](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/29.aspx).
Negative Mitzvah 169: That the tribe of Levi shall not take a portion in the Land: [105](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/105.aspx).

## Seder Admur

Tzitzis, after having made the upper knot properly: [199](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/199.aspx).

Before and without a doubt, from the beginning of the month... until the 12th of the month, inclusive, etc.: [1](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/1/1/1.aspx). [4](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/1/1/4.aspx).

Sefiras HaOmer: one should have in mind the count of that night and one word of Ana B'Koach, etc.: [11](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/11.aspx).

## רדב"ז, שו"ת

_Section: רדב"ז, שו"ת_

**Hebrew:**

ח"ג א'נב (תרנז) אם יש ספק סכנות נפשות הרי"ז חסיד שוטה דספיקא דידי' עדיף כו': [128](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/128.aspx).
אלף שכז טעם שאין מברכים שהחיינו בספה"ע: [9](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/9.aspx).
ח"ד א'תקפב (ריח) [לשונות הרמב"ם]: בדין להכניס עצמו בספק סכנה בכדי להציל אחרים: [128](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/128.aspx).

**English:**

## Radbaz, Responsa

Vol. 3, 152 (5757): Regarding whether one who enters a situation of potential danger to life is considered a "pious fool" (chassid shoteh), and whether his own doubt takes precedence, etc..

1027: The reason why we do not recite Shehecheyanu upon counting Sefiras HaOmer..

Vol. 4, 1582 (218) [Language of the Rambam]: Regarding the law of placing oneself into a situation of potential danger in order to save others..

---


## דרוש וחידוש (רעק"א)

_Section: דרוש וחידוש (רעק"א)_

**Hebrew:**

**כתובות**
לג, ב ד"ה יכולני: הטעם שרוצח שיצא חוץ לעיר מקלטו כל אדם אין חייבים עליו:129.
**חינוך**
מצוה רפד ואת קדשי בנ"י לא תחללו גו' זו היא מניעה שלא לאכול מעשר ראשון בטבלו: [66](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/2/66.aspx).
מצוה שו ויש שאמרו כו' כולן מצוה אחת היא כו': [10](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/10.aspx).
לפי שכל עיקרן של ישראל אינו אלא התורה כו' נצטוינו למנות ממחרת כו' וכל חפצו להגיע אל הזמן ההוא: [14](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/14.aspx).
מצוה של ספירת זבה אינו אלא השגחה בימים כו' ולא שיתחייבו למנותם בפה: [15](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/15.aspx).

**English:**

## Drush V’Chiddush (R’ Akiva Eiger)

**Kesuvos**
33b, s.v. Yacholni: The reason that if a murderer leaves his city of refuge, anyone is not liable for him [for killing him]. 

**Chinuch**
Mitzvah 284: "And you shall not profane the holy things of the Bnei Yisrael, etc." — this is a prohibition against eating *maaser rishon* while it is *tevel*. 
Mitzvah 306: "And there are those who say, etc." — all of them are one mitzvah, etc. 
Because the entire essence of Yisrael is nothing but the Torah, etc., we were commanded to count from the morrow, etc., and his entire desire is to reach that time. 
The mitzvah of counting for a *zavah* is nothing but an observation of the days, etc., and not that they are obligated to count them verbally.

---


## יד מלאכי

_Section: יד מלאכי_

**Hebrew:**

**כללי הרמב"ם**
ס"ב אין דרכו לכתוב ענינים מחודשים כו': [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).
אות ב' וה' דרכו של הרמב"ם להעתיק דיני התלמוד כלשונם: [30](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/30.aspx).
**כללי הסמ"ג**
סמ"ו הסמ"ג דרכו תמיד להלוך בעקבות הרמב"ם כו': [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).

**English:**

## Rules of the Rambam
Section 62: It is not his custom to write novel concepts, etc..
Letters 2 and 5: It is the custom of the Rambam to transcribe the laws of the Talmud exactly as they are phrased..

## Rules of the Sefer Mitzvos Gadol (Smag)
Section 546: The Smag’s custom is always to follow in the footsteps of the Rambam, etc..

## מנחת חינוך

_Section: מנחת חינוך_

**Hebrew:**

מצוה צח [תמי' על הרמב"ן שכ' שמקשה מעכב גם לדורות]: [34](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/34.aspx).
מצוה שו [השקו"ט בדין עבד שנשתחרר וקטן שהגדיל באמצע ימי הספירה]: [10](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/10.aspx).
מצו שסד תשובה אינה מצוה: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
מצוה תח לעתיד לבוא יתנו להם [לויים] ערים . . דגם לעת"ל לא יטלו הלויים ג"כ נחלה כו': [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).
[הג' אומות הם ג"כ בכלל ארצות שנכרתה ברית לאברהם כו']: [106](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/106.aspx).
מצוה תי [בטעם שהגולה אינו יוצא מעיר מקלטו אפילו לפקו"נ]: [128](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/128.aspx).
מצוה תקה ודבר זה [שלעת"ל נוטלין הלוים חלק בארץ] צ"ע דלעת"ל יתבטלו שני המצות: [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).
הג' אומות הם ג"כ בכלל ארצות שנכרתה ברית לאברהם: [106](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/106.aspx).
מצוה תקכ לשיטת הסמ"ג . . דלעת"ל נוטלים הלויים חלק בארץ בוודאי לא יתנו ישראל ערים להם: [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).

**English:**

## Minchas Chinuch

Mitzvah 98 [A query regarding the Ramban, who writes that the *mekasheh* (the one who brings the offering) is a requirement even for future generations]: [34](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/34.aspx).
Mitzvah 306 [The back-and-forth discussion regarding the law of a slave who was emancipated and a minor who reached maturity during the days of the Sefirah]: [10](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/10.aspx).
Mitzvah 364 [Teshuvah is not a mitzvah]: [18](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/18.aspx).
Mitzvah 378 [In the future to come, they will give the Levites cities . . . for even in the future to come, the Levites will likewise not take an inheritance, etc.]: [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).
[The three nations are also included in the lands for which a covenant was made with Avraham, etc.]: [106](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/106.aspx).
Mitzvah 410 [Regarding the reason that the exile does not leave his city of refuge even for the sake of saving a life]: [128](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/128.aspx).
Mitzvah 415 [And this matter—that in the future to come the Levites will take a portion in the land—requires further study, for in the future to come, these two mitzvos will be nullified]: [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).
The three nations are also included in the lands for which a covenant was made with Avraham: [106](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/106.aspx).
Mitzvah 520 [According to the opinion of the Smag . . . that in the future to come the Levites will take a portion in the land, surely Yisrael will not give them cities]: [104](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/104.aspx).

## צפנת פענח

_Section: צפנת פענח_

**Hebrew:**

**אמור**
ס"פ [החילוק בין כהנים ולוים בירושת הארץ לעת"ל]: [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).
**שלח**
יג, ג [רצון המרגלים באופן קנין הארץ]: [48](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/48.aspx).
יג, כ [טעם ע"ד ההלכה לוהתחזקתם ולקחתם מפרי הארץ]: [48](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/48.aspx).
**קרח**
יח, כ בארצם לא תנחל כו' ר"ל אף בקיני קניזי קדמוני לא כמו שבט לוי כו': [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).
**מטות**
לב, מא על פרש"י: לפי שלא היו לו בנים כו': [119](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/119.aspx).
**הוספות**
דברים בהוספות (לפ' מקץ) ע' שמג — כולם נזירים כמו נזיר שמעון הצדיק וזה יהי' לאחר תחה"מ כו': [32](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/32.aspx).
**מכות**
יא, ב בטעם שהגולה אינו יוצא מעיר מקלטו אפילו לפקו"נ ובגדר איסור היציאה חוץ לערי מקלט: [128](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/128.aspx). [130](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/130.aspx).
**אדר"נ**
פ"ל יצא חוץ מן מקלטו במזיד . . אין הטעם משום המיתה רק זה דין מחמת שיצא מן המקלט: [129](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/129.aspx).
**רמב"ם הל' תפילין**
פ"ד ה"ד [בתש"י העיקר הפעולה, ובתש"ר העיקר הנפעל]: [50](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/50.aspx).
**רמב"ם הל' מאכא"ס**
דף פה, ב [אם נזירות הוא רק איסור גברא]: [28](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/28.aspx).
**רמב"ם הל' נדרים**
דף יז, ב אם נזירות הוא איסור גברא או חפצא: [28](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/28.aspx).
**רמב"ם הל' נזירות**
בתחילתו אם נזירות הוא דבר עצמי . . או הוא אוסר עצמו בהני דברים: [28](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/28.aspx).
דף יח, ג גבי נדר אף דהוא איסור חפצא מ"מ יש עליו גם איסור גברא: [29](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/29.aspx).
**רמב"ם הל' ערכין**
פ"א הי"ג כיון שיכול לחזור לעיר מקלטו אין עליו שם גברא קטילא: [130](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/130.aspx).
בסופן דבר שאין לו קצבה אינו יכול . . הא צדקה ג"כ יש לה קצבה עד חומש: [112](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/2/112.aspx).

**English:**

## צפנת פענח

**Emor**
End of the parsha [The distinction between Kohanim and Leviim regarding the inheritance of the Land in the time to come]: [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).

**Shelach**
13:3 [The intent of the Meraglim regarding the manner of acquiring the Land]: [48](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/48.aspx).
13:20 [The reason according to Halacha for "and you shall strengthen yourselves and take from the fruit of the Land"]: [48](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/48.aspx).

**Korach**
18:20 "In their land you shall not inherit, etc." — meaning, even in the lands of the Kenite, Kenizzite, and Kadmonite, unlike the tribe of Levi, etc.: [107](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/107.aspx).

**Matos**
32:41 Regarding Rashi’s commentary: "Because he had no sons, etc.": [119](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/119.aspx).

**Hosafos**
Devarim in the Hosafos (to Parshas Mikeitz) p. 343 — they will all be Nazirites like the Nazirite of Shimon HaTzaddik, and this will be after the resurrection of the dead, etc.: [32](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/32.aspx).

**Makkos**
11b Regarding the reason that a manslayer does not leave his city of refuge even for the sake of saving a life, and the parameters of the prohibition of leaving the cities of refuge: [128](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/128.aspx). [130](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/130.aspx).

**Avos D'Rabbi Nasan**
Chapter 30: If he left his place of refuge intentionally... the reason is not because of the death penalty, but rather this is a decree because he left the place of refuge: [129](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/129.aspx).

**Rambam, Hilchos Tefillin**
Chapter 4, Halacha 4 [Regarding Tefillin shel Yad, the essence is the action; regarding Tefillin shel Rosh, the essence is the object acted upon]: [50](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/50.aspx).

**Rambam, Hilchos Ma'achalos Assuros**
Page 85b [Whether Naziriteship is merely a personal prohibition (*issur gavra*)]: [28](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/28.aspx).

**Rambam, Hilchos Nedarim**
Page 17b: Whether Naziriteship is a personal prohibition (*issur gavra*) or a prohibition upon the object (*issur cheftza*): [28](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/28.aspx).

**Rambam, Hilchos Neziros**
At the beginning: Whether Naziriteship is an essential matter... or whether he prohibits himself from these things: [28](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/28.aspx).
Page 18c: Regarding vows, even though it is a prohibition upon the object (*issur cheftza*), nevertheless there is also a personal prohibition (*issur gavra*) upon him: [29](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/29.aspx).

**Rambam, Hilchos Arachin**
Chapter 1, Halacha 13: Since he can return to his city of refuge, he does not bear the status of a "dead man" (*gavra katila*): [130](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/2/130.aspx).
At the end: A matter that has no limit cannot be [vowed]... yet Tzedakah also has a limit, up to a fifth: [112](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/2/112.aspx).

## קהלת יעקב

_Section: קהלת יעקב_

**Hebrew:**

**מע' אש מתלקחת ומע' ענן גדול ומע' רוח סערה**
[אש ענן רוח הם בינה זו"ן דקליפה]: [161](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/161.aspx).
**ע' ד' קליפות**
ג' קליפות חג"ת נה"י מל' דקליפה, וק"נ א"ס וכח"ב כו': [161](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/161.aspx).

**English:**

## The Appearance of a Flaring Fire, the Appearance of a Great Cloud, and the Appearance of a Stormy Wind

**The appearance of a flaring fire, the appearance of a great cloud, and the appearance of a stormy wind**
[Fire, cloud, and wind are the Binah and ZON of the kelipah]:.

**The appearance of the four kelipos**
The three kelipos are the Chesed, Gevurah, Tiferes, Netzach, Hod, Yesod, and Malchus of the kelipah, while the Keter, Chochma, and Binah are [from the side of] the Ein Sof, and so on:.

סי' ו' אות י"ז אם ב"נ מצווה על לא יחל דברו בנדר ובשבועה: [27](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/27.aspx).

**English:**

**Klalim, Maareches Samech**
Klal 63: Whether a matter derived through logical reasoning (*sevara*) is considered to have the status of *d’oraisa*: [30](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/30.aspx).

**Pe’as HaSadeh, Klalim, Maareches Gimmel**
Siman 6, Os 17: Whether a *ben Noach* is commanded regarding the prohibition of "he shall not profane his word" (*lo yacheil dvaro*) regarding vows and oaths: [27](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/27.aspx).

---


## של"ה

_Section: של"ה_

**Hebrew:**

**חלק תושבע"פ מס' שבועות**
קפא, א בכל דיבור ודיבור של רש"י יש בו . . ענינים מופלאים: [124](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/1/124.aspx).
**חלק תושב"כ**
ר"פ וישב המועדים . . בכולן יש שייכות לאותן הפרשיות שחלות בהן: [124](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/1/124.aspx).

**English:**

## Oral Torah Section: Shavuos

In every single utterance of Rashi, there are wondrous matters [124](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/1/124.aspx).

## Written Torah Section

At the beginning of Parshas Vayeishev, the festivals... all of them have a connection to the specific parshiyos that fall out during those times [124](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/1/124.aspx).

**English:**

## תשובות בעלי התוס' מכת"י

See the responsa of the Maharam of Rothenburg: "He places a neshamah that is worthy of being a Yid into the womb of a non-Jew, and that person becomes a ger."

## כתר שם טוב

_Section: כתר שם טוב_

**Hebrew:**

סמ"ג לפי מחשבתו של אדם . . כך עוברים לפניו בגשמי כו': [64](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/64.aspx).
סרט"ז מחשבה . . יכול לבטלו: [64](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/64.aspx).
סרפ"ה כאשר . . יכול להשיג מחשבת חבירו באופן שהוא רוצה כמו כו': [64](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/6/1/64.aspx).

**English:**

## Kesser Shem Tov

Sefer Mitzvos Gadol: According to a person’s thoughts... so do they pass before him in the physical, etc..

Sefer Tziyoni: Thought... can nullify it..

Sefer Reishis Chochma: When... one can grasp the thought of his fellow in the manner that he desires, etc..

## Tanya

Chapter 2: A literal portion of Elokus from above. [73](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/73.aspx)
Chapter 4: The 613 limbs of the soul. [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx)
In the place of His greatness, etc. [43](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/43.aspx)
Chapter 6: The Shechinah only rests where, etc. Even one... Shechinah... every group of ten, etc. [43](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/43.aspx)
All the affairs of this world are difficult... and the wicked prevail within it. [24](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/24.aspx)
And it is called in the Chariot of Yechezkel a stormy wind and a great cloud, etc. [160](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/160.aspx)
Chapter 7: This world... the majority of it is evil, etc. [24](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/24.aspx)

Chapter 10: Who is a Chassid? One who acts with kindness toward his Creator, etc. [45](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/45.aspx)
Chapter 12: The brain rules over the heart, etc. (and notes and corrections). [101](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/3/101.aspx)

[Based on "And Hashem commanded us all these statutes to fear Hashem"]. [73](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/73.aspx)

Chapter 37: The ultimate perfection of the Messianic era and the resurrection of the dead depends on our deeds and our avodah throughout the duration of the exile. [100](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/8/3/100.aspx)
The soul itself requires no rectification at all, etc. [77](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/77.aspx)
Chapter 38: [The primary drawing down of mitzvos is through speech and action more than through thought]. [20](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/20.aspx)
Tefillah or any other blessing without kavanah is like a body without a soul. [52](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/52.aspx)
Chapter 42: Moshe Rabbeinu... is one of the seven shepherds, etc., and Moshe Rabbeinu is the inclusion of them all, etc. [193](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/193.aspx)

**English:**

## Torah Or

[192](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/192.aspx) (In Torah Or, it is sometimes explained even according to opinions that are not accepted as halacha).
1, 2 Through refining his deeds . . his mind and heart become clear, etc.: [149](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/2/149.aspx).
19, 3 From the ancient nations . . they abandon all pleasures, etc.: [31](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/2/31.aspx).
20, 2 [The virtue of the joy of a mitzvah]: [204](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/9/204.aspx).
29, 1 [During the day he would only light the western candle, etc.]: [192](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/192.aspx).
29, 3 That between the evenings he lights all seven candles, and in the morning, at the time of the cleaning of the two candles, etc.: [192](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/192.aspx).
Mitzvos that are in physical action are in the category of ketores, etc.: [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).
40, 2 and onwards [based on "And Hashem will illuminate my darkness," light that comes from darkness]: [120](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/120.aspx).
43, 2 Air is in the category of letters . . "a mitzvah is a candle," etc.: [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).
83, 1 Tzitz is from the expression "his crown shall blossom" (yatzitz), "peering (metzitz) through the lattices," etc.: [200](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/200.aspx).
84, 1 Tzitz is a masculine term . . tzitzis is a feminine term, etc.: [200](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/200.aspx).
96, 3 His Essence and Being, may He be blessed, commanded and they were created . . automatically, etc.: [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).

צב, א נוגה הוא הממוצע . . והוא מ"ש במרכבת יחזקאל רוח סערה כו': [160](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/160.aspx).
צד, ד וירד הגבול . . התורה היא בשיעורים וגבולים כו' וע"י כו': [125](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/1/125.aspx).

###### ואתחנן

ט, ד­י, א מצוות . . צריכים שמירה כו': [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).

###### ראה

כ, א מצוות צריכות שמירה כו': [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).
כ, ג עצמותו ומהותו ית' צוה ונבראו . . ממילא כו': [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).
לב, ב מלך . . בשדה כו' מקבל את כולם בספ"י כו': [195](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/195.aspx).

###### נצבים

מד, א כל ישראל קומה אחת שלימה שכולם מתאספין כו' להיות לאחדים כאחד: [164](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/164.aspx).
מה, ג­ד תשובה . . במדריגה עליונה יותר מכל המצות . . למלאות הפגם והחסרון כו': [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

###### ראש השנה

נט, ד כתיב יתקע ולא נזכר מי התוקע כו': [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).

###### האזינו

עד, ד [ע"ד עבודת האופנים]: [121](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/121.aspx).

###### שמע"צ

פה, א תשובה ומעשים טובים דהיינו . . טובים ומאירים כו': [24](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/24.aspx).
צא, ג בזמן שאין ביהמ"ק קיים הוא מציץ מן החרכים כו': [199](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/199.aspx).

###### ברכה

צז, ב [בענין בן כרך ובן כפר]: [121](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/121.aspx).
צח, א המקום והזמן שניהם הם נבראים בבחי' אחת: [15](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/15.aspx).

###### שה"ש

יז, ג תשובה ומעשים טובים . . טובים שיהיו מאירים כו': [24](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/24.aspx).
כג, ג מצחא . . מבחי' כי לא אדם כו': [200](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/200.aspx).
כד, א [דרגות אתעדל"ת ואתעדל"ע]: [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).
מח, א­ב לעתיד . . תורה חדשה . . בחי' נישואין . . התגלות כו': [227](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/12/227.aspx).

**English:**

## Likutei Torah

### Vayikra
1, 1: It is not mentioned at all in the verse who the caller was [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).

### Kedoshim
30, 2: "And I looked, and behold, a stormy wind..." and in the holy *sefer* it is explained, etc. [160](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/160.aspx).

### Emor
36, 2: "And you shall count for yourselves from the morrow of the Shabbos, etc." — the drawing down of the *makifim* of *Imma*, etc., which are above Shabbos, etc. [144](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/2/144.aspx).

### Behar
41, 2: They occupy space... also in the aspect of time; both are created in one aspect [15](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/15.aspx).

### Bamidbar
13, 1: *Mitzvos*... the limbs of the *Melech*, etc. The Torah is the aspect of the blood... which draws the life-force into the limbs [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

### Beha'aloscha
Beginning of the *parsha*: Aharon... is one of the seven shepherds, etc. [193](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/193.aspx).
30, 1: "Who is a *Chassid*? One who acts with kindness toward his Creator, etc." [45](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/2/45.aspx).

### Shelach
37, 1: They did not want to lower themselves to physical *mitzvos*, etc. [52](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/52.aspx).
38, 2-3: They did not want to enter *Eretz Yisrael*... physical *asiyah*... they were mistaken that the main thing is to perform them in the Land... "the land is good," etc. [52](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/5/1/52.aspx).

### Chukas
60, 1: The three *kelipos* that are impure, mentioned in the Chariot of Yechezkel: "a stormy wind, a great cloud, and a fire flashing up" [160](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/160.aspx).
65, 4: "Thick air"... in order to illuminate, etc. [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).

### Balak
70, 3-4: *Tefillah*... is not counted among the *mitzvos*... it is like the analogy of the spinal cord, etc. [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

### Pinchas
80, 2: It is not hinted at in any letter or *kotz*, etc. [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).

### Masei
88, 3-89, 2: "These are the journeys"... plural form, etc. To exit the aspect of *Mitzrayim*... and therefore all the forty-two journeys, etc. [224](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/12/224.aspx).
92, 1: *Noga* is the intermediary... and this is what is stated in the Chariot of Yechezkel: "a stormy wind," etc. [160](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/160.aspx).
94, 4: "And the border shall descend"... the Torah is in measurements and boundaries, etc., and through, etc. [125](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/11/1/125.aspx).

### Va'eschanan
9, 4-10, 1: *Mitzvos*... require guarding, etc. [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).

### Re'eh
20, 1: *Mitzvos* require guarding, etc. [185](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/185.aspx).
20, 3: His *Atzmus* and *Mahus* (may He be blessed) commanded, and they were created... automatically, etc. [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).
32, 2: "The King... in the field," etc. He receives everyone with a smiling countenance, etc. [195](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/5/195.aspx).

### Nitzavim
44, 1: All of *Klal Yisrael* are one complete stature, as they all gather together, etc., to become unified as one [164](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/3/164.aspx).
45, 3-4: *Teshuvah*... is on a higher level than all the *mitzvos*... to fill the flaw and the deficiency, etc. [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

### Rosh Hashanah
59, 4: It is written "He shall sound," but it is not mentioned who is doing the sounding, etc. [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).

### Ha'azinu
74, 4: [Regarding the *avodah* of the *Ofanim*]. [121](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/121.aspx).

### Shemini Atzeres
85, 1: *Teshuvah* and good deeds, meaning... good and illuminating, etc. [24](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/24.aspx).
91, 3: At a time when the *Beis Hamikdash* does not exist, He "peeks through the lattices," etc. [199](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/199.aspx).

### Beracha
97, 2: [Regarding the matter of a city-dweller and a villager]. [121](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/10/1/121.aspx).
98, 1: Space and time, both are created in one aspect [15](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/2/1/15.aspx).

### Shir HaShirim
17, 3: *Teshuvah* and good deeds... good, that they should be illuminating, etc. [24](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/24.aspx).
23, 3: "Forehead"... from the aspect of "For He is not a man," etc. [200](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/6/200.aspx).
24, 1: [Levels of *is'arusa d'lesata* and *is'arusa d'le'eila*]. [38](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/4/1/38.aspx).
48, 1-2: In the future... a new Torah... the aspect of marriage... revelation, etc. [227](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/12/12/227.aspx).

## מאמרי אדהאמ"צ

_Section: מאמרי אדהאמ"צ_

**Hebrew:**

###### דברים ח"א

ע' ד ואילך [ג' אומות וז' אומות מוחין ומדות]: [108](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/108.aspx).
ע' שלה תשובה נמנה מצוה . . לכפר . . במנין המצות: [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

###### נ"ך

ע' לח­ט כל ההשתלשלות הוא רק כמו טפה בים . . ולא כמו שכתבו . . בטלה במציאותה כו':124.

###### דרושי חתונה ח"א

ע' קלא ומשיח יתקיים בגופו עם שרש נשמתו למטה כמו שהוא למעלה ממש כו': [74](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/74.aspx).

**English:**

## Devarim Vol. 1

See page 4 and onwards [The three nations and the seven nations, Mochin and Midos]: [108](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/9/1/108.aspx).
See page 335, Teshuvah is counted as a mitzvah . . to atone . . in the enumeration of the mitzvos: [22](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/3/1/22.aspx).

## Nach

See page 38-39, the entire Seder Hishtalshelus is merely like a drop in the ocean . . and not as they have written . . nullified in its existence, etc.: 124.

## Drushei Chassunah Vol. 1

See page 131, and Moshiach will exist in his body with the root of his neshamah below, just as he is above, literally, etc.: [74](@apppath/admur/lkus/38/7/1/74.aspx).
